; -- 72A3
72A3    LD A,($FC0A)    
72A6    AND $80 
72A8    RET Z   
72A9    LD HL,$FC0E                         ; set HL to FC0E and wait until after next interrupt
72AC    HALT                                ;
72AD    LD A,($FC0D)                        ; loop interrupt waiting 256 - FC0D times
72B0    INC A                               ; .
72B1    JR NZ,$72AC                         ; .
72B3    HALT                                ; wait for an interrupt again
72B4    LD A,($FC0D)                        ; if FC0D = 255 loop around to interrup again
72B7    CP $FF                              ; .
72B9    JR Z,$72B3                          ; .
Note on each call here A is updated with the result of the xor or flip operations
it looks like none move HL on but do change its value
72BB    CP $42                              ; case A = 01100110  flip bit 5 of (HL) return in A
72BD    CALL Z,$7304                        ; .
72C0    CP $44                              ; case A = 01000100  fip bit 3 of (HL) return in A
72C2    CALL Z,$730A                        ; 
72C5    CP $46                              ; case A = 01000110  flip bit 6 of HL return in A
72C7    CALL Z,$7310                        ;
72CA    CP $4B                              ; case A = 01001011  Xor HL with (72A2) if any of the lower 2 bits of HL are set and return with A = 0 (so skipping follow on tests and force the play sound one)
72CC    CALL Z,$7331                        ; 
72CF    CP $51                              ; case A = 01010001 HL = ABS(HL), A = 0 (also clear bit 7 of hl)
72D1    CALL Z,$7316                        ; 
72D4    CP $52                              ; case A = 01010010 fip bit 2 of (HL) return in A
72D6    CALL Z,$731C                        ; 
72D9    CP $53                              ; case A = 01010011 52 set bit 7 of (HL) return in A
72DB    CALL Z,$7322                        ;
72DE    CP $59                              ; case A = 01011001 fip bit 5 of (HL) and save into 7128 as well as return in A
72E0    CALL Z,$732B                        ;
72E3    CP $31                              ; case A = 01001001 FC08 to FC0C = 0, carry set, don't do any more tests
72E5    JR Z,$72FF                          ;
72E7    CP $20                              ; case A = 00110010 FC08 to FC0C = 0, carry clear, don't do any more tests
72E9    JR Z,$72F1                          ;
72EB    AND A                               ; case A = 0 play sound
72EC    CALL Z,$7344    
72EF    JR $72AC    
;--72F1
72F1    LD HL,$FC08                 ; FC08 to FC0C = 0, carry clear
72F4    XOR A   
72F5    LD (HL),A   
72F6    INC HL  
72F7    LD (HL),A   
72F8    INC HL  
72F9    LD (HL),A   
72FA    INC HL  
72FB    LD (HL),A   
72FC    INC HL  
72FD    LD (HL),A   
72FE    RET 
; 
72FF    CALL $72F1                  ; FC08 to FC0C = 0, carry set
7302    SCF                         ; 
7303    RET 
; -- 7304 flip bit 5 of (HL) and return value in A
7304    LD A,(HL)                   ; flip bit 5 of (HL)
7305    XOR $10                     ;
7307    LD (HL),A                   ;
7308    XOR A                       ;
7309    RET                         ; Done

;-- 8080 Draw a screen buffer with single pixel line left right and bottom to memory location 80D1 - (126 * 32) to 80D1
; Screen buffer looks to be
; 126 lines of 32 characters
; 4032 bytes from C040 to $D000
;
;

8080    DI                              ; no interrups
8081    LD ($80D1),SP                   ; save stack to 80D1
8085    LD SP,$D000                     ; stack is now D000 or 53248
8088    LD HL,$0000                     ;
808B    LD DE,$00FF                     ;
808E    LD IX,$FF00                     ;
8092    LD BC,$FFFF                     ;
8095    PUSH DE                         ; fill memory 
8096    LD A,$0E                        ; .      
8098    PUSH BC                         ; .      
8099    DEC A                           ; .      80BE with 1
809A    JR NZ,$8098                     ; .      80BF with 0   
809C    PUSH IX                         ; .      80C0 with 0
809E    LD E,$01                        ; .      80C1 to 80D0 with FF
80A0    LD IX,$8000                     ; .      80D1 with 0
80A4    LD B,$7E                        ; . loop in groups of 32 bytes (i.e. 1 screen line) walking back from 80BD?
80A6    PUSH DE                         ; .      00 80 00.......00 00 01 00
80A7    PUSH HL                         ; . do this for 126 times (i.e lines)
80A8    PUSH HL                         ; . 
80A9    PUSH HL                         ; . I suspect 80BE is a buffer for the screen
80AA    PUSH HL                         ; .
80AB    PUSH HL                         ; .
80AC    PUSH HL                         ; .
80AD    PUSH HL                         ; .
80AE    PUSH HL                         ; .
80AF    PUSH HL                         ; .
80B0    PUSH HL                         ; .
80B1    PUSH HL                         ; .
80B2    PUSH HL                         ; .
80B3    PUSH HL                         ; .
80B4    PUSH HL                         ; .
80B5    PUSH IX                         ; .
80B7    DJNZ $80A6                      ; .
80B9    LD BC,$FFFF                     ; finish off with pushing one last line of FF FF..... FF 00 ( I suspect a solid line)
80BC    LD E,$FF                        ; .
80BE    LD IX,$FF00                     ; .
80C2    PUSH DE                         ; .
80C3    LD A,$0E                        ; .
80C5    PUSH BC                         ; .
80C6    DEC A                           ; .
80C7    JR NZ,$80C5                     ; .
80C9    PUSH IX                         ; .
80CB    LD SP,($80D1)                   ; recover stack 
80CF    EI  
80D0    RET                             ; return

;   this is a sound routine as it works on buts 4 and 3 of port $FE , i.e. the speaker, plays 64 bytes, D seems to be the delay factor E could be number of loops?

; A098 I think this is BHL = AHL + DE where AHL = 16 bit + A sign and DE = 15 bit signed
A098    LD B,A                          ; B = A , C = D (save sign bytes)
A099    LD C,D                          ; .
A09A    XOR C                           ; A = A xor C
A09B    RES 7,D                         ; clear sign bit of D

A09F    ADD HL,DE                       ; HL = HL + DE
A0A0    RET                             ; return 
A0A1    SBC HL,DE                       ; HL = HL -DE
A0A3    RET NC                          ; if no carry return
A0A4    ADD HL,DE                       ; else HL = HL + DE
A0A5    EX DE,HL                        ;      swap HL and DE
A0A6    AND A                           ;      reset carry
A0A7    SBC HL,DE                       ;      HL = DE - HL (as they were swapped)
A0A9    LD B,C                          ;      B = sign of C
A0AA    RET                             ;      ret

A115    ADD A,C                         ; A = A + C                                     (3E)

A123    RL E                            ; e = e * 2                                     (70)
A125    RRA                             ; A = A / 2                                     (1F)

Example data

    -06 -05 -04 -03 -02 -01
     00  09  2D  7F  12  BB
61Ef is a matrix  but also backwards 
    +00 +01 +02 +03 +04 +05  
     2B  00  3F  16  BB  45
     
     
; -- AA10
; A is two 4 bit offsets fetched against A984 table, if the lower half does not return a value try with upper half
AA10    LD B,A                          ; B = A
AA11    SRL B                           ; B = A / 8
AA13    SRL B                           ;
AA15    SRL B                           ;
AA17    SRL B                           ; B = upper 4 bits of A in lower half of B
AA19    AND $0F                         ; A = lower 8 bits of A
AA1B    CALL $AA20                      ; 
AA1E    RET NZ                          ; if AA20 returned non zero then exit as we have a value 
AA1F    LD A,B                          ; A = upper 8 bits of A as lower
AA20    LD HL,$A984                     ; HL = A984 + A 
AA23    ADD A,L                         ;
AA24    LD L,A                          ;
AA25    JR NC,$AA28                     ;
AA27    INC H                           ;
AA28    LD A,(HL)                       ; a = (A984 + A) or A = (984 + A/8)
AA29    AND A                           ; clear carry flag 
AA2A    RET 
; -- AA2B                               
AA2B    LD A,($A9C8)                    ; A = (A9C8)
AA2E    AND A                           ; if a <> 0 goto AA8B
AA2F    JR NZ,$AA8B                     ;
AA31    LD A,(IX+$00)                   ; if (IX) != (IX - 6) goto AA8B
AA34    CP (IX-$06)                     ; .
AA37    JR NZ,$AA8B                     ; 
AA39    LD A,(IX+$01)                   ; if (IX+1) != (IX -5) goto AA8V
AA3C    CP (IX-$05)                     ;
AA3F    JR NZ,$AA8B                     ;
AA41    LD A,(IX+$02)                   ; if (IX+2) != (IX -4) goto AA8V
AA44    CP (IX-$04)                     ;
AA47    JR NZ,$AA8B                     ;
AA49    LD A,(IX+$03)                   ; B = A = (IX+3) XOR (IX -3)
AA4C    XOR (IX-$03)                    ; 
AA4F    LD B,A                          ; 
AA50    LD L,(IY+$12)                   ; HL = IY + [12 13]
AA53    LD H,(IY+$13)                   ;
AA56    LD E,(IY+$14)                   ; DE = IY + [14 15]
AA59    LD D,(IY+$15)                   ;
AA5C    XOR H                           ; H = A = sign bit of (A XOR (IY + 13))
AA5D    AND $80                         ;
AA5F    LD H,A                          ;
AA60    LD (IY+$13),H                   ; (IY + $13) = A
AA63    RL B                            ; A = B *= 2 (and moves bit 7 to carry)
AA65    LD A,B                          ; 
AA66    XOR D                           ; (IY + $15) = D = A = sign bit of A xor D
AA67    AND $80                         ;
AA69    LD D,A                          ; 
AA6A    LD (IY+$15),D                   ;
AA6D    CALL $AAFB                      ; A = L (signH) + E (signD)
AA70    LD L,A                          ; L = L (signH) + E (signD)
AA71    LD E,(IY+$16)   
AA74    LD D,(IY+$17)   
AA77    LD A,B  
AA78    RLA 
AA79    XOR D   
AA7A    AND $80 
AA7C    LD D,A  
AA7D    LD (IY+$17),D   
AA80    CALL $AAFB                      ; A = L (signH) + E (signD)
AA83    LD L,A  
AA84    LD DE,$0006 
AA87    ADD IY,DE   
AA89    JR $AAE3                        ; JP3 >>
AA8B    LD B,(IX+$00)   
AA8E    CALL $AB1E  
AA91    LD A,(IX+$03)   
AA94    XOR (IY+$01)    
AA97    RLA 
AA98    RR H    
AA9A    LD (IY+$12),L   
AA9D    LD (IY+$13),H   
AAA0    EX DE,HL    
AAA1    INC IY  
AAA3    INC IY  
AAA5    LD B,(IX+$01)   
AAA8    CALL $AB1E  
AAAB    LD A,(IX+$03)   
AAAE    RLA 
AAAF    XOR (IY+$01)    
AAB2    RLA 
AAB3    RR H    
AAB5    LD (IY+$12),L   
AAB8    LD (IY+$13),H   
AABB    CALL $AAFB                      ; A = H(sgn)L + D(sign)E
AABE    LD L,A  
AABF    EX DE,HL    
AAC0    INC IY  
AAC2    INC IY  
AAC4    LD B,(IX+$02)   
AAC7    CALL $AB1E  
AACA    LD A,(IX+$03)   
AACD    RLA 
AACE    RLA 
AACF    XOR (IY+$01)    
AAD2    RLA 
AAD3    RR H    
AAD5    LD (IY+$12),L   
AAD8    LD (IY+$13),H   
AADB    CALL $AAFB                      ; A = H(sgn)L + D(sign)E
AADE    LD L,A  
AADF    INC IY  
AAE1    INC IY  
AAE3    LD A,($A9C7)                    ; JP3 <<
AAE6    LD B,A  
AAE7    XOR A   
AAE8    LD C,H  
AAE9    RES 7,H 
AAEB    SRL H   
AAED    RR L    
AAEF    RRA 
AAF0    DJNZ $AAEB  
AAF2    JR NC,$AAF5 
AAF4    INC HL  
AAF5    BIT 7,C 
AAF7    RET Z   
AAF8    SET 7,H 
AAFA    RET 
; -- AAFB   A = H(sgn)L + D(sign)E
AAFB    LD A,H                          ; if signs H & D are the same
AAFC    XOR D                           ; .
AAFD    RLA                             ; .
AAFE    JR C,$AB03                      ; .
AB00    LD A,L                          ;    then H(sgn)A = L + E
AB01    ADD A,E                         ;    .
AB02    RET                             ;    .
AB03    LD A,L                          ;    else H(sgn)A = Sign D ABS(L - E)
AB04    SUB E                           ;   
AB05    RET NC                          ;    
AB06    NEG                             ;
AB08    AND A                           ;
AB09    LD H,D                          ;
AB0A    RET                             ;
; -- AB0B -- A = $BF00 [B + C)/2] - $BF00 [ABS(B-C)/2]                 ; is this log arithim?
AB0B    LD A,B                          ; A = ABS(B - C)               ( in our example A = FA)
AB0C    SUB C                           ; .                            ( A = FA - 0C = EE with no carry)
AB0D    JR NC,$AB11                     ; .
AB0F    NEG                             ; .
AB11    SRL A                           ; L = A = A /2                  (A = 77 so HL = $BF77 so D becoms £37)
AB13    LD H,$BF                        ; H = $BF00 + A/2                   
AB15    LD L,A                          ;      
AB16    LD D,(HL)                       ; D = $BF00 [ABS(B-C)/2]       ( this may be a log arithim table)
AB17    LD A,B                          ; L = A = (B + C) / 2          ( L = A = FA + 0C = 06 with carry, RRA to 83)
AB18    ADD A,C                         ; .           
AB19    RRA                             ; .
AB1A    LD L,A                          ; .       
AB1B    LD A,(HL)                       ; A = $BF00 [B + C)/2]
AB1C    SUB D                           ; A = $BF00 [B + C)/2] - $BF00 [ABS(B-C)/2)] (in our exampl HL=$BF83 so A = 'C' - '7' so 0C
AB1D    RET                             ; ret
; -- AB1E
AB1E    LD A,($A9C7)    
AB21    SLA B   
AB23    DEC A   
AB24    JR NZ,$AB21 
AB26    LD C,(IY+$01)   
AB29    RES 7,C 
AB2B    PUSH DE 
AB2C    CALL $AB0B  
AB2F    LD L,A  
AB30    LD H,$00    
AB32    POP DE  
AB33    RET 
;-- AB34        - I think all incomming values are X 2
AB34    LD A,B                          ; E = $BE00 [ABS(B - C)*2]
AB35    SUB C                           ; .
AB36    JR NC,$AB3A                     ; .
AB38    NEG                             ; .
AB3A    SRL A                           ; .
AB3C    LD H,$BE                        ; .
AB3E    LD L,A                          ; .
AB3F    LD E,(HL)                       ; .
AB40    INC H                           ; D = $BF00 [ABS(B - C)*2]   
AB41    LD D,(HL)                       ;
AB42    DEC H                           ; A = $BE00 [B + C)/2]
AB43    LD A,B                          ; .
AB44    ADD A,C                         ; . 
AB45    RRA                             ; .
AB46    LD L,A                          ; .
AB47    LD A,(HL)                       ; .
AB48    INC H                           ; H = $BF00 [$BE00 [B + C)/2]
AB49    LD H,(HL)                       ; .
AB4A    LD L,A                          ; L = A
AB4B    AND A                           ; clear carry
AB4C    SBC HL,DE                       ; HL = HL - DE
AB4E    RET                             ;
; -- AB4F   AHL = BHL + DE signed where BHL is 16 bit sign byte DE = 15 bit signed
AB4F    LD C,D                          ; C = D
AB50    RL E                            ; DE = DE * 2 clearing sign bit
AB52    RL D                            ; .
AB54    LD A,B                          ; A = B XOR C (so B xor D)
AB55    XOR C                           ; 
AB56    JR NZ,$AB5B                     ; if not zero got AB5B
AB58    ADD HL,DE                       ; HL = HL + DE (i.e. HL = HL + DE*2 for a Dword offset
AB59    LD A,B                          ; A = B
AB5A    RET                             ; return
AB5B    SBC HL,DE                       ; HL = HL - DE (ie. HL = HL - DE * 2)
AB5D    JR NC,$AB66                     ; if HL < DE
AB5F    ADD HL,DE                       ;    HL = HL + DE
AB60    EX DE,HL                        ;    swap DE an HL
AB61    AND A                           ;    Clear carry
AB62    SBC HL,DE                       ;    HL = HL - DE (so in effect if HL < DE then HL = DE - HL
AB64    LD A,C                          ;    A = C
AB65    RET                             ;
AB66    LD A,H                          ; else
AB67    OR L                            ;    if HL = 0
AB68    LD A,C                          ;       A = C (or D sign), HL = 0
AB69    RET Z                           ;    else
AB6A    POP DE                          ;       get stack top 4 bytes
AB6B    POP AF                          ;       .
AB6C    NEG                             ;       neg (now that will set carry of A <> 0
AB6E    PUSH AF                         ;       put top 4 bytes back on stack
AB6F    PUSH DE                         ;       .
AB70    DEC HL                          ;       HL = HL - 1
AB71    LD A,B                          ;       A = B
AB72    RET                             ;
;-- this looks like a matrix calc
AB73    LD A,($A9C8)    
AB76    AND A   
AB77    PUSH IX 
AB79    JR NZ,$AB9F 
AB7B    LD B,$03    
AB7D    LD A,(IX+$00)                   ; if IX + 0 <> IX - 6 goto $AB9F
AB80    CP (IX-$06) 
AB83    JR NZ,$AB9F 
AB85    INC IX  
AB87    DJNZ $AB7D  
AB89    POP IX  
AB8B    CALL $ABC0                      ; looks like it processes row 1
AB8E    LD ($A9BB),HL                   ; A9BB = result in HL
AB91    CALL $ABC0                      ; looks like it processes row 2
AB94    LD ($A9BD),HL                   ; A9BD = result in HL
AB97    CALL $ABC0                      ; looks like it processes row 3
AB9A    LD ($A9BF),HL                   ; A9BD = result in HL
AB9D    JR $ABB3    
AB9F    POP IX                          l
ABA1    CALL $AC01                      ; this may be mulitply the row?
ABA4    LD ($A9BB),HL   
ABA7    CALL $AC01  
ABAA    LD ($A9BD),HL   
ABAD    CALL $AC01  
ABB0    LD ($A9BF),HL   
ABB3    XOR A   
ABB4    LD ($AC9F),A    
ABB7    LD ($ACA0),A    
ABBA    LD ($ACA1),A    
ABBD    JP $ACDF    
;-- ABC0
; looks like A 7 to 5 are 3 sign bits
; driving y = y +/- x and z = z +/- (y +/- x), moved IY on to next row of a 3 x2 byte matrix
ABC0    LD A,(IX+$03)               ; A = IX+3 xor IX-3  (so likley an X and Y sign )
ABC3    XOR (IX-$03)    
ABC6    LD B,A                      ; B = sign xor
ABC7    LD L,(IY+$12)               ; HL = IY + 12,13 L = value H = sign
ABCA    LD H,(IY+$13)   
ABCD    LD E,(IY+$14)               ; de = IY + 14,15 E = value D = sign
ABD0    LD D,(IY+$15)   
ABD3    XOR H                       ; sign xor H sign
ABD4    AND $80                     ; retainting bit 7
ABD6    LD H,A                      ; IY+13  = sign of A xor H
ABD7    LD (IY+$13),H               ;
ABDA    RL B                        ; move B bit 7 into carry flag B *= 2
ABDC    LD A,B                      ; A = B

AFE2    AND A                           ;   .

AFEC    RET Z                           ;
AFED    SET 7,H                         ; else set H negative bit

; -- B3A7
B3A7    LD A,B                  ; A = (B / 2) xor  B
B3A8    SRL A                   ; .
B3AA    SRL A                   ; .
B3AC    XOR B                   ; 
B3AD    ADD A,A                 ; A = A * 16
B3AE    ADD A,A                 ;
B3AF    ADD A,A                 ;
B3B0    ADD A,A                 ;
B3B1    OR B                    ; A = A or B or 3
B3B2    OR $03                  ;
B3B4    LD B,A                  ; B = A,
B3B5    RES 5,B                 ; clear bit 5 of B
B3B7    AND $20                 ; D = A AND $20
B3B9    LD A,D                  ; 
B3BA    JR Z,$B3C7              ; if A <> 0
B3BC    BIT 3,B                 ;    test bit 3 of B
B3BE    JR Z,$B3C2              ;    if it was set
B3C0    SET 5,B                 ;       set bit 5 of B
B3C2    ADD A,H                 ;       A = A + H
B3C3    JR NC,$B3DA             ;       if A +H < 256 goto B3DA
B3C5    JR $B3DC                ;       else goto B3DC
B3C7    SUB H                   ; A = A - H 
B3C8    JR C,$B3D2              ; if H <= A
B3CA    BIT 3,B                 ;   if bit 3 of B is set
B3CC    JR Z,$B3DA              ;          
B3CE    SET 5,B                 ;      set bit 5 of B
B3D0    JR $B3DA                ;      go to B3DA
B3D2    NEG                     ; else negate A
B3D4    BIT 3,B                 ;      if bit 3 of B is set
B3D6    JR NZ,$B3DA             ;
B3D8    SET 5,B                 ;         set bit 5 of B
B3DA    RES 1,B                 ; B3DA:clear bit 1 of B
B3DC    LD H,A                  ; h = A
B3DD    BIT 4,B                 ; test bit 4 of B
B3DF    LD A,E                  ; A = E
B3E0    RES 4,B                 ; clear bit 4 of B
B3E2    JR Z,$B3EF              ; if bit 4 of B was set
B3E4    BIT 2,B                 ;    test bit 2 of B
B3E6    JR Z,$B3EA              ;    if bit 2 of B was set
B3E8    SET 4,B                 ;       set bit 4 of B
B3EA    ADD A,L                 ;    A = A + L  
B3EB    JR NC,$B402             ;    if A > L goto B402
B3ED    JR $B404                ;    else     goto B404
B3EF    SUB L                   ; else A = A -l 
B3F0    JR C,$B3FA              ; if A > L
B3F2    BIT 2,B                 ;    if bit 2 of B was set
B3F4    JR Z,$B402              ;       set bit 4 of B
B3F6    SET 4,B                 ;       
B3F8    JR $B402                ;       goto B402 
B3FA    NEG                     ; else negate A
B3FC    BIT 2,B                 ;      if bit 2 B is clear
B3FE    JR NZ,$B402             ;      then
B400    SET 4,B                 ;         set bit 4 of A
B402    RES 0,B                 ; B402:reset bit 4 of A
B404    LD L,A                  ;

B872    JP Z,$BBBA                  ; if A = 0 goto BBBA                                              So look up jump table bnased on lower 4 bits of A
B875    DEC A                       ; else A = A - 1                                                  A = 0     BBBA
B876    JP Z,$B96B                  ;      if A = 0 goto B96B                                         A = 1     B96B
B879    DEC A                       ;      else A = A - 1                                             A = 2     B99F
B87A    JP Z,$B99F                  ;          if A = 0 goto B99F                                     A = 3     return and do nothing
B87D    DEC A                       ;          else A = A - 1                                         A = 4     B9E7
B87E    RET Z                       ;          if A = 0 return                                        A = 5     BA94
B87F    DEC A                       ;          else A = A - 1                                         A = 6     BAF2
B880    JP Z,$B9E7                  ;               if A = 0 goto B9E7                                A = 7     BAFA
B883    DEC A                       ;               else A = A - 1                                    A = 8     BA4D
B884    JP Z,$BA94                  ;                    if A = 0 goto BA94                           A = 9     VV75
B887    DEC A                       ;                    else A--                                     A = 10 to 15 return and do nothing 
B888    JP Z,$BAF2                  ;                         if A = 0 goto BAF2                      
B88B    DEC A                       ;                         else A--                                
B88C    JP Z,$BAFA                  ;                              if A = 0 goto BAFA

B890    JP Z,$BB4D                  ;                                    if A = 0 goto BA4D           
B893    DEC A                       ;                                    else A--                     
B894    JP Z,$BB75                  ;                                         if A = 0 goto BB75

DB8E    JP $DAE1    
; DB91 Clear bit sign bit of D0BD for 10 Dwords
DB91    LD B,$0A                        ; for HL = D0DB to D0EC in DWord steps
DB93    LD HL,$D0BD                     ;     clear bit7 of (HL)
DB96    RES 7,(HL)                      ; (i..e clear bit 7 of 0A DWORDS 
DB98    INC HL                          ;
DB99    INC HL                          ;
DB9A    DJNZ $DB96                      ;
DB9C    XOR A                           ; (DA76) = A
DB9D    LD ($DA76),A                    ;
DBA0    RET                             ; Done
DBA1    NOP 
; -- DBA2 -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
DBA2    LD HL,$FC0A                     ; A = (FC0A) retaining bits 5 and 4
DBA5    LD A,(HL)                       ; return if FC0A bits 4 and 5 were clear
DBA6    AND $30                         ;
DBA8    RET Z                           ; 
DBA9    LD B,A                          ; b = A
DBAA    LD A,(HL)                       ; clear bits 5 and 4 of (FC0A)
DBAB    AND $CF                         ; 
DBAD    LD (HL),A                       ;
DBAE    LD A,($DBA1)                    ; if (DBA1) = 0 then return
DBB1    AND A                           ;
DBB2    RET NZ                          ;
DBB3    LD A,($7104)                    ; if (7104) <> 0
DBB6    AND A                           ;
DBB7    JR Z,$DC0A                      ;
DBB9    BIT 5,B                         ;    else if Bit 5 of (FC0A) was clear goto DBCF
DBBB    JR Z,$DBCF                      ;
DBBD    BIT 4,B                         ;         then if bit 4 of (FC0A) was clear return
DBBF    RET Z                           ;
DBC0    LD A,($D08D)                    ;              else if (D0D8) = 0 then return
DBC3    AND A                           ;               
DBC4    RET Z                           ;
DBC5    LD A,$02                        ;                   else (D03F) = 2
DBC7    LD ($D03F),A                    ;
DBCA    LD BC,$7406                     ;                         BC = 7406
DBCD    JR $DBEB                        ;
DBCF    CALL $DF60                      ;         else call DF60
DBD2    LD HL,($DEF6)                   ;              hl = (DEF6)
DBD5    LD A,H                          ;              if H <> 0
DBD6    AND A                           ;              Then
DBD7    JR NZ,$DC04                     ;              
DBD9    LD A,L                          ;              
DBDA    AND A                           ;                if L = 0
DBDB    RET Z                           ;                   return
DBDC    LD B,A                          ;                else 
DBDD    LD A,($D082)                    ;                     A = (D082) - L
DBE0    SUB B                           ;
DBE1    JR C,$DC04                      ;                     if (D082) < L goto DC04
DBE3    LD A,$01                        ;                     else 
DBE5    LD ($D03F),A                    ;                         (D03F) = 1

; it looks like draw two lines down the screen E52B width appart for row C to Row c + E52B rows at postition Col A

E665    LD A,($D052)                    ;    .

E671    LD B,A                          ;       
E672    JR $E683                        ; else

FBF7    JR NZ,$FC46 
FBF9    CALL P,$5943    
FBFC    LD L,$2E    
FBFE    LD L,$00    
FC00    NOP 
FC01    NOP 
FC02    NOP 
FC03    NOP                                                                                 ; y = FC08 $86
FC04    NOP                                                                                 ; v = FC44 $12 (changes jump address)
FC05    NOP                                                                                 ;
FC06    NOP                                                                                 ;
FC07    NOP                                                                                 ;
; FC08 - keystate map, looks to be 5 bytes of 8 bits                                        ;
?                                          bit map  7  6  5  4  3  2  1  0                  > p = data on system 
FC08    NOP             ; keystate byte 0                 7  O  P     L                     > S = dive X = climb o = Short range
                                                    Y              Y  Y
                                                    Z              Z  Z
FC09    NOP             ; keystate byte 1                    Sp S  X  M  N                  >
FC0A    NOP             ; keystate byte 2                 G  H  4  3  2  1                  > 1 = front view 2 = read 3 = left 4 = right
FC0B    NOP             ; keystate byte 3                 B     C  F                        > space accellerate ? C = 8?
FC0C    NOP             ; keystate byte 4                 D                                 >
                                                       B  B  B
                                                       R  R
; -- FC0D Keypressed variable
FC0D    RST $38 
FC0E    ADC A,H         ; I think this is joystick input state
; FC08 - keystate map byte 7
;                                          bit map  7  6  5  4  3  2  1  0                  > p = data on system 
FC0F    NOP             ; keystate byte 7                    7  6  8  5  9
                                                             
; FC10 - Back end of keyboard loop
FC10    DEC D           ; D = D -1
FC11    JP NZ,$FD76     ; if D > 0 goto KeyboardReadLoop
FC14    LD A,($FC09)    ; else D = lower 4 bits of (FC09) 
FC17    AND $0F         ; .
FC19    LD D,A          ; .
FC1A    LD A,($FC0E)    ;      E = lower 3 bits of (FC0E)
FC1D    LD E,A          ;      .
FC1E    AND $03         ;      if E <> 0 
FC20    JR Z,$FC63      ;     
FC22    DEC A           ;         A = A - 1
FC23    JR NZ,$FC3D     ;         IF A = 0
FC25    LD BC,$FF1F     ;            Read port Kempston joystick port
FC28    IN A,(C)        ;            if fire pressed (read into A)
FC2A    BIT 4,A         ;            .
FC2C    JR Z,$FC33      ;            .
FC2E    LD HL,$FC0B     ;               set bit 0 of keystate byte 3
FC31    SET 0,(HL)      ;            end if
FC33    AND $0F         ;            clear fire bit of A
FC35    LD D,A          ;            D = A
FC36    LD A,E          ;            E by here is lower 3 bits of FC0E
FC37    XOR $30         ;            Flip bits 6 to 5 of E
FC39    LD E,A          ;
FC3A    JP $FC63        ;         else
FC3D    DEC A           ;            A = A - 1 (note to generate Z flag?)
FC3E    LD A,($FC0F)    ;            D = (FC0F) / 2 (rra does not affect Z but will set carry as appropriate)
FC41    RRA             ;            bit 0 of FC0F to carry
FC42    LD D,A          ;              
FC43    JR Z,$FC57      ;            if A <> 0 (basically copy bits from A to D skipping bit 0 and reversing order)
FC45    LD D,$00        ;               D = 0
FC47    RL D            ;               set bit 5 of D to bit 1 of FC0F
FC49    RRA             ;               skip bit 2 of FC0F
FC4A    RRA             ;               set bit 4 of D to bit 3 of FC0F
FC4B    RL D            ;                 
FC4D    SLA D           ;               skip bit 3 of D
FC4F    RRA             ;               set bit 2 of D to bit 4 of FC0F
FC50    RR D            ;                 
FC52    RRA             ;               set bit 1 of D to but 5 of FC0F
FC53    RL D            ;                 
FC55    RL D            ;               move all up by 1 bit skipping but 0
FC57    LD HL,$FC08     ;            if bit 6 of FC08 is set
FC5A    BIT 6,(HL)      ;
FC5C    JR Z,$FC63      ;
FC5E    LD HL,$FC0B     ;               then set bit 0 of keystate byte 3
FC61    SET 0,(HL)      ;            end if
FC63    BIT 4,E         ;      if bit 4 of E (FC0E) is set
FC65    JR Z,$FC74      ;         C = first 5 bits of (D * 2)
FC67    LD A,D          ;         .
FC68    AND $05         ;         .
FC6A    SLA A           ;         .
FC6C    LD C,A          ;         .
FC6D    LD A,D          ;         A = D bits 3 and 1 moved into bits 2 and 0
FC6E    AND $0A         ;         .
FC70    SRL A           ;         .
FC72    OR C            ;         D = A or first 4 bits of D * 2
FC73    LD D,A          ;         .
FC74    BIT 5,E         ;         .
FC76    JR Z,$FC89      ;         if 5 of E FC0E) is set 
FC78    LD A,D          ;
FC79    AND $03         ;
FC7B    LD B,A          ;
FC7C    LD A,D          ;
FC7D    AND $0C         ;
FC7F    LD C,A          ;
FC80    SRL C           ;
FC82    SLA A           ;
FC84    OR C            ;
FC85    AND $0C         ;
FC87    OR B            ;
FC88    LD D,A          ;
FC89    LD HL,$FC09 
FC8C    LD A,($FC0E)    ; A = (FC0E) lower 2 bits (left and right?)
FC8F    AND $03 
FC91    JR NZ,$FCA1 
FC93    LD A,(HL)   
FC94    AND A   
FC95    JR Z,$FCA1  
FC97    INC L   
FC98    RES 7,(HL)  
FC9A    INC L   
FC9B    RES 2,(HL)  
FC9D    RES 7,(HL)  
FC9F    DEC L   
FCA0    DEC L   
FCA1    LD A,(HL)                   ; READING FC09
FCA2    AND $F0 
FCA4    OR D    
FCA5    LD (HL),A   
FCA6    LD HL,$FC08 
FCA9    BIT 6,(HL)  
FCAB    RET Z   
FCAC    RES 6,(HL)  
FCAE    LD A,($FC0A)    
FCB1    AND $80 
FCB3    RET Z   
FCB4    LD A,$FE    
FCB6    LD ($FC0D),A    
FCB9    RET 
; -- FCBA Respond to keypress and updates keystate table FC08
FCBA    PUSH BC                     ; save BC and AF
FCBB    PUSH AF                     ;                                                                                ; example 7 key gets ascii $37 
FCBC    LD A,$05                    ; A= 5 - key number from FD7E (5 down to 1)                                      ; A = 3 so A ends up 1B 
FCBE    SUB E                       ; .                                                                              ;          and B ends up $36
FCBF    SLA A                       ; A = A * 8                                                                      ;fetch 37 from $FD41 + 1B
FCC1    SLA A                       ;                                                                                ;      and savein FC0D
FCC3    SLA A                       ;                                                                                ;fetch A = FC from FF58 + $36
FCC5    ADD A,D                     ; A = A + D - 1 (D is row counter for keyboard)                                  ;      B = 10 from FF59 + $36
FCC6    DEC A                       ; .                                                                              ;fetch A = FF58 + FC
FCC7    LD B,A                      ; B = A * 2                                                                      ;      = 0
FCC8    SLA B                       ;                                                                                ;      or FC08 with $10 from B
FCCA    LD HL,$FD41                 ; HL = FD41 + A                                                                  ;      
FCCD    ADD A,L                     ; . fast version as its only 16 bit + 8 bit                                      ;
FCCE    JR NC,$FCD1                 ; .                                                                              ;
FCD0    INC H                       ; .                                                                              ;
FCD1    LD L,A                      ; .                                                                              ;
FCD2    LD A,(HL)                   ; (FC0D) = (FD41) offset keyboard map ASCII code                                 ;
FCD3    LD ($FC0D),A                ; .                                                                              ;
FCD6    LD HL,$FF58                 ; HL = FF58 + B                                                                  ;
FCD9    LD A,L                      ; .                                                                              ;
FCDA    ADD A,B                     ;                                                                                ;
FCDB    LD L,A                      ;                                                                                ;
FCDC    LD A,(HL)                   ; A = (HL) - keystate byte, B = (HL + 1) mask of other keys in byte              ;
FCDD    INC HL                      ;                                                                                ;
FCDE    LD B,(HL)                   ;                                                                                ;
FCDF    LD HL,$FC08                 ; A = (FC08 + A) I think this is the keystate table                              ;
FCE2    ADD A,L                     ;
FCE3    LD L,A                      ;
FCE4    LD A,(HL)                   ;
FCE5    OR B                        ; or with B mask
FCE6    LD (HL),A                   ; save back into (FC08 + A)
FCE7    POP AF                      ; recover AF and BC
FCE8    POP BC                      ;
FCE9    RET                         ; Done

; FD41  to FE65 keyboard bit and port to ASCII table
is start of row to key table shoudl be 8 * 5 bytes
20 0D 50 30 31 51 41 00 01 4C 4F 39 32 57 53 5A
4D 4B 49 38 33 45 44 58 4E 4A 55 37 34 52 46 43
42 48 59 36 35 54 47 45
so it runs bit per row, port per column

   Space    Enter   P   0   1   Q   A Shift
   Sym      L       O   9   2   W   A   Z
   M        K       I   9   3   E   D   X
   N        J       U   7   4   R   F   C
   B        H       Y   6   5   T   G   V

KeyboardReadLoop:
FD76    RLC B                       ; Shift B right  (7FFE -> FEFE)
FD78    IN A,(C)                    ; A = read keyboard port
FD7A    AND $1F                     ; mask so only bits 1 to 5 are selected
FD7C    XOR $1F                     ; invert bits so that 1 for keypress 0 for not press
FD7E    LD E,$05                    ; for E = 0 to 5
FD80    RRA                         ;   move a left 1 bit so carry holds key press
FD81    CALL C,$FCBA                ;   if key was pressed call FCBA -- FCBA Respond to keypress and updates keystate table FC08
FD84    DEC E                       ; next E
FD85    JR NZ,$FD80                 ; .
FD87    JP $FC10                    ;

; i thin kthis is updating delta roll and pitch from joystick or keyboard
FE01    if (70E3) >= 4 then return
        b = (FC09)  ; keystate byte 1
        c = (FC0E)  ; poss joystick?
        
        if bit 0 of FF08 is set
           if bit 1 of B is clear and HL <> 0
              if hl > 0
                 if bit 2 of c is set
                    hl = 0
                 else
                    if ABS(hl - 255) < 8192
                       then hl = hl - 255
                       else hl = 0
                 end if
              else
                if hl + 255 < 2048 and > -2045
                   hl = hl + 255
                end if
           end if
        else
           if bit 1 of FF08 is set and ABS(HL) <> 0
              if H > 0 and ABS(HL + 255) < 2048
                 then hl = hl + 255
              else
                 if bit 2 of C is set
                    hl = 0
                 else
                    if (ABS(hl - 255) < 8192
                       hl = hl - 255
                    else 
                       hl = 0
                    end if
                 end if
             end if
           end if
        end if
        (FF08) = HL
         hl = (FF0A)
         .. updates FF0A basd on bits and limits at FEE8
FEEB:   HL = (FF0C)
        de = $A0
        if bit 4 of B is clear
           if bit 5 of B is set
              HL = MAX(HL - $0A,0)
        else
           if bit 5 of B is clear
              if ( ABS(HL + 0A) < 4096)
                 HL = MIN(HL + 0A,0)?
FF1D   (FF0C) = hl
       (FC09) = 0
       ret
